SET SQL_MODE = "NO_AUTO_VALUE_ON_ZERO";
START TRANSACTION;
SET time_zone = "+00:00";

CREATE DATABASE `cinema_booking_system`;
use `cinema_booking_system`;

--
-- Cơ sở dữ liệu: `cinema_booking_system`
--

DELIMITER $$
--
-- Các hàm
--
CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` FUNCTION `check_suatchieu` (`suatchieu_check` TIME, `phongchieu_check` INT, `ngaychieu_check` DATE, `duration_check` INT) RETURNS INT(11)  BEGIN
    IF EXISTS(
        SELECT * FROM suatchieu sc 
        JOIN phim p ON sc.id_phim = p.id_phim 
        WHERE sc.id_phongchieu = phongchieu_check
        AND sc.date_show = ngaychieu_check
        AND sc.deleted = 0
        AND ((suatchieu_check BETWEEN time_show AND ADDTIME(time_show, SEC_TO_TIME(p.duration * 60)))
        OR (ADDTIME(suatchieu_check, SEC_TO_TIME(duration_check * 60)) BETWEEN time_show AND ADDTIME(time_show, SEC_TO_TIME(p.duration * 60))))
    ) THEN
        RETURN 0;
    ELSE 
        RETURN 1;
    END IF;
END$$

DELIMITER ;

--
-- Cấu trúc bảng cho bảng `khachhang`
--

CREATE TABLE `khachhang` (
  `id_khachhang` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `name` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `email` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `phone` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `birthday` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `pass` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  `avatar_path` text DEFAULT 'user.png',
  `point` int(11) DEFAULT 0
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci;

--

--
-- Cấu trúc bảng cho bảng `phongchieu`
--

CREATE TABLE `phongchieu` (
  `id_phongchieu` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `sohang` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `id_rap` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `name_phongchieu` text NOT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci;

--
-- Đang đổ dữ liệu cho bảng `phongchieu`
--

INSERT INTO `phongchieu` (`id_phongchieu`, `sohang`, `id_rap`, `name_phongchieu`) VALUES
(16, 7, 1, 'Phòng 1'),
(17, 7, 2, 'Phòng 1'),
(18, 6, 1, 'Phòng 3'),
(19, 5, 1, 'Phòng 2'),
(20, 6, 2, 'Phòng 2'),
(21, 5, 3, 'Phòng 1'),
(22, 6, 1, 'Phòng 4'),
(23, 5, 3, 'Phòng 2'),
(24, 5, 2, 'Phòng 3'),
(25, 6, 3, 'Phòng 3');

--
-- Bẫy `phongchieu`
--
DELIMITER $$
CREATE TRIGGER `tr_insert_ghe` AFTER INSERT ON `phongchieu` FOR EACH ROW BEGIN
    DECLARE i INT DEFAULT 1;
    WHILE i <= NEW.sohang DO
        INSERT INTO ghe (id_phongchieu, hangghe, vitri)
        VALUES (NEW.id_phongchieu, i, 1), (NEW.id_phongchieu, i, 2), (NEW.id_phongchieu, i, 3), (NEW.id_phongchieu, i, 4), (NEW.id_phongchieu, i, 5), (NEW.id_phongchieu, i, 6), (NEW.id_phongchieu, i, 7), (NEW.id_phongchieu, i, 8), (NEW.id_phongchieu, i, 9), (NEW.id_phongchieu, i, 10), (NEW.id_phongchieu, i, 11), (NEW.id_phongchieu, i, 12), (NEW.id_phongchieu, i, 13), (NEW.id_phongchieu, i, 14);
        SET i = i + 1;
    END WHILE;
END
$$
DELIMITER ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Cấu trúc bảng cho bảng `rap`
--

CREATE TABLE `rap` (
  `id_rap` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `name` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `address` text DEFAULT NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci;

--
-- Đang đổ dữ liệu cho bảng `rap`
--

--
-- Bẫy `suatchieu`
--
DELIMITER $$
CREATE TRIGGER `tr_suatchieu_insert` AFTER INSERT ON `suatchieu` FOR EACH ROW BEGIN
  INSERT INTO suatchieu_ghe (id_suatchieu, id_ghe)
  SELECT NEW.id_suatchieu, g.id_ghe FROM ghe g
  WHERE g.id_phongchieu = NEW.id_phongchieu;
END
$$
DELIMITER ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Cấu trúc bảng cho bảng `suatchieu_ghe`
--

CREATE TABLE `suatchieu_ghe` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `id_suatchieu` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `id_ghe` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `trangthai` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci;
